<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">LAS
VEGAS, January 12, 2026 /PRNewswire/ &mdash; (NYSE AMERICAN: BMNR) Bitmine Immersion Technologies, Inc. (&ldquo;Bitmine&rdquo; or the
&ldquo;Company&rdquo;) a Bitcoin and Ethereum Network Company with a focus on the accumulation of crypto for long term investment, today
announced Bitmine crypto <I>+ total cash + &ldquo;moonshots&rdquo; </I>holdings totaling $14.0 billion.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">As
of January 11th at 7:00pm ET, the Company&rsquo;s crypto holdings are comprised of 4,167,768 ETH at $3,119 per ETH (Coinbase), 193 Bitcoin
(BTC), $23 million stake in Eightco Holdings (NASDAQ: ORBS) (&ldquo;moonshots&rdquo;) and total cash of $988 million. Bitmine&rsquo;s
ETH holdings are 3.45% of the ETH supply (of 120.7 million ETH).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;2026
augurs many positive things for crypto with stablecoin adoption and tokenization driving to make blockchain the settlement layer of Wall
Street, particularly favoring Ethereum,&rdquo; said Thomas &ldquo;Tom&rdquo; Lee of Fundstrat, Chairman of Bitmine. &ldquo;We continue
to view the leverage reset post October 10th, 2025 as akin to the &lsquo;mini crypto winter.&rsquo; 2026 is the year crypto prices recover
and with stronger gains in 2027-2028.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;In
the past week, we acquired 24,266 ETH and still managed to increase our cash position by $73 million,&rdquo; continued Lee. &ldquo;Bitmine
only issues equity selectively and only at a premium to mNAV. We remain the largest &lsquo;fresh money&rsquo; buyer of ETH in the world,&rdquo;
stated Mr. Lee. &ldquo;And when MAVAN launches its commercial operations, we will be the largest staking provider in the entire crypto
ecosystem.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Bitmine
released a special Chairman&rsquo;s message (<U>link</U>) explaining why Bitmine stockholders should vote to support the amendment to
increase authorized shares ahead of the upcoming annual stockholder meeting on January 15, 2026 (the &ldquo;Annual Meeting&rdquo;).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;Bitmine
charter has an unusual feature requiring 50.1% of all shares outstanding to support a share increase. This is an extremely high bar and
thus, makes it very difficult to get an authorized share increase. We need to pursue this increase now as Bitmine is soon to exhaust
its current 500 million authorization. And when that happens, our ETH accumulation will slow. Thus, we need stockholders to approve proposal
#2 to increase authorized shares,&rdquo; said Tom Lee. &ldquo;Bitmine&rsquo;s sole focus remains creating stockholder value, achieving
this by accretively acquiring ETH per share, and has only issued shares at mNAV premium, optimizing yield and income on its ETH holdings,
and strategically investing the balance sheet on &lsquo;moonshots&rsquo; and leveraging the company&rsquo;s strong community and market
position to generate additional returns.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">As
of January 11, 2026, Bitmine total staked ETH stands at 1,256,083 ($3.9 billion at $3,119 per ETH). This is an increase of 596,864 in
the past week. This is a fraction of the 4.17 million ETH held by Bitmine. The CESR (composite Ethereum staking rate, administered by
<U>Quatrefoil</U>) is 2.81%. Bitmine is currently working with 3 staking providers as the company moves towards unveiling its commercial
MAVAN (Made in America VAlidator Network) in 2026. &ldquo;Bitmine has staked more ETH than other entities in the world.&rdquo;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&ldquo;At
scale (when Bitmine&rsquo;s ETH is fully staked by MAVAN and its staking partners), the ETH staking fee is $374 million annual (using
2.81% CESR), or greater than $1 million per day,&rdquo; stated Tom Lee. &ldquo;We continue to make progress on our staking solution known
as The Made in America Validator Network (MAVAN). This will be the &lsquo;best-in-class&rsquo; solution offering secure staking infrastructure
and will be deployed in early calendar 2026,&rdquo; continued Lee.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Bitmine
crypto holding reigns as the #1 Ethereum treasury and #2 global treasury, behind Strategy Inc. (MSTR), which owns 672,497 BTC valued
at $61 billion. Bitmine remains the largest ETH treasury in the world.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Bitmine
is now one of the most widely traded stocks in the US. According to data from Fundstrat, the stock has traded average daily dollar volume
of $1.3 billion (5-day average, as of January 9, 2026), ranking #67 in the US, behind Vistra (rank #66) and ahead of Cisco (rank #68)
among 5,704 US-listed stocks (<U>statista.com</U> and Fundstrat research).</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The
GENIUS Act and Securities and Exchange Commission&rsquo;s (the &ldquo;SEC&rdquo;) Project Crypto are as transformational to financial
services in 2025 as US action on August 15, 1971 ending Bretton Woods and the USD on the gold standard 54 years ago. This 1971 event
was the catalyst for the modernization of Wall Street, creating the iconic Wall Street titans and financial and payment rails of today.
These proved to be better investments than gold.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
Bitmine</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><U>Bitmine</U>
(NYSE AMERICAN: BMNR) is the leading Ethereum Treasury company in the world, implementing an innovative digital asset strategy for institutional
investors and public market participants. Guided by its philosophy of &ldquo;the alchemy of 5%,&rdquo; the company is committed to ETH
as its primary treasury reserve asset, leveraging native protocol-level activities including staking and decentralized finance mechanisms.
The company will launch MAVAN (Made-in America Validator Network), a dedicated staking infrastructure for Bitmine assets, in Q1 of 2026.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0pt; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

additional details, follow on X:</FONT></P>
